2026-07-16 | Fire 77 — process lesson: highest-ever single-fire scout-dedup-failure rate | KB-process note, not a finding | Of ~13 "new" candidates reported across the VC-portfolio, HKEX-A1, Korea-DART, and Chinese-trade-press scouts this fire, 9 were already-known/already-killed and caught only at orchestrator synthesis (Laifu Harmonic, KH Vatec, Robotis, Samhyun, Samgi, Global SM, ITM Semiconductor, Xinjian Transmission/Seenpin, Benmo Power) — a ~70% false-positive rate on "new" claims, matching and possibly exceeding the Fire 61 record (~72%). This is the identical category error (passenger-ADAS counted as AV/humanoid thesis exposure) that removed Seyond one fire ago. Genuinely-qualifying robotaxi+humanoid revenue (Zoox/Motional/Pony.ai/WeRide/Baidu/DiDi + Unitree/HONOR Robot/Galbot/Magiclab/Vita Dynamics, all primary-sourced) is an estimated single-digit-to-low-teens % of total revenue, not the ~90%+ implicitly assumed by the carried 7/8 score. Opus re-derivation: Gate 1 (not-re-rated) 0.5/2, Gate 2 (named buyer) 1.5/2, Gate 3 (multiplies/capture-rate) 1/2, Gate 4 (financial health) 2/2 — total ≈5/8. Bear/base/bull (qualifying-segment-driven whole-stock price): $9-12/$14-19/$28-40. Unlike Seyond, HSAI keeps a real, primary-sourced qualifying-buyer roster and is GAAP-profitable (~$1B net cash) — earns a monitor slot rather than a strict REMOVE; a stricter TARGET-PROFILE reading (>$500M cap, <15% exposure, >10yr old, ADAS-driven) would justify full removal. D.C. Circuit 25-5256 (still no ruling ~4mo post-argument) and the Aug-28 EGM (record date confirmed 07-23, circular still unpublished) remain binding for the STOCK PRICE but are now secondary for thesis-fit classification. Flips back up on: robotics/robotaxi+humanoid revenue disclosed separately >20-25% AND >100% growth, or an 8-figure humanoid contract. Flips further down on: confirmation qualifying revenue is <10% and flat/shrinking, continued RoboSense robotics-lidar share gains, or an adverse court ruling.
